     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    54→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    77→
    78→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    79→        .filter(c => {
    80→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    81→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    82→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    83→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    84→        })
    85→        .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
    86→
    87→      const systemPrompt =
    88→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    89→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    90→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    91→
    92→      const userPrompt =
    93→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    94→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    95→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    96→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    97→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
    98→        `Choose one action:
` +
    99→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   100→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   101→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   102→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_name", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   103→
   104→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   105→
   106→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   107→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   108→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   109→        model: this.model,
   110→        max_tokens: 256,
   111→        system: systemPrompt,
   112→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   113→      });
   114→
   115→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   116→
   117→      if (!res.ok) {
   118→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   119→        return;
   120→      }
   121→
   122→      const data = await res.json();
   123→
   124→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   125→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   126→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   127→              ?? null;
   128→
   129→      if (!text) {
   130→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   131→        return;
   132→      }
   133→
   134→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   135→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   136→    } catch (err) {
   137→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   138→    } finally {
   139→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   140→    }
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   144→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   145→
   146→    switch (decision.action) {
   147→      case 'move':
   148→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   149→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   150→        }
   151→        break;
   152→
   153→      case 'interact': {
   154→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   155→        if (obj) {
   156→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   157→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   158→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   159→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   160→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        break;
   164→      }
   165→
   166→      case 'idle':
   167→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   168→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   169→        break;
   170→
   171→      case 'talk': {
   172→        const target = characters.find(c => c.name === decision.targetCharacter);
   173→        if (target) {
   174→          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
   175→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   176→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   177→            // Character B responds when A arrives
   178→            if (decision.targetDialogue) {
   179→              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
   180→            }
   181→            // Queue conversation event for the debug log
   182→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   183→              simState.pushEvent({
   184→                type: 'conversation',
   185→                speakerLabel: character.label,
   186→                targetLabel: target.label,
   187→                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   188→                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
   189→              });
   190→            }
   191→          }
   192→        }
   193→        break;
   194→      }
   195→    }
   196→
   197→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   198→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   199→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    if (decision.description) {
   203→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   204→    }
   205→
   206→    if (this.onDecision) {
   207→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   208→    }
   209→  }
   210→}

SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}
   305→

USERMESSAGE #25
✓ TOOL RESULT

     1→/**
     2→ * speechBubble.js — creates a transient speech bubble above a Phaser sprite.
     3→ *
     4→ * Usage:
     5→ *   showSpeech(scene, sprite, "Hello!");
     6→ *
     7→ * The bubble fades out automatically after ~3 seconds. No teardown needed.
     8→ */
     9→
    10→const BUBBLE_PAD   = 7;   // px padding inside bubble
    11→const BUBBLE_MAX_W = 150; // max bubble width (word-wrap threshold)
    12→const BUBBLE_R     = 6;   // corner radius
    13→const TRI_H        = 8;   // triangle pointer height
    14→const DISPLAY_MS   = 2500; // ms before fade starts
    15→const FADE_MS      = 600;  // fade duration
    16→
    17→export function showSpeech(scene, sprite, text) {
    18→  // ── Text object ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    19→  const txt = scene.add.text(0, 0, text, {
    20→    fontSize: '10px',
    21→    color: '#1a1a1a',
    22→    fontFamily: 'monospace',
    23→    wordWrap: { width: BUBBLE_MAX_W - BUBBLE_PAD * 2 },
    24→  })
    25→    .setOrigin(0.5, 0)
    26→    .setDepth(21);
    27→
    28→  const bw = Math.min(txt.width + BUBBLE_PAD * 2, BUBBLE_MAX_W);
    29→  const bh = txt.height + BUBBLE_PAD * 2;
    30→
    31→  // Position: above the sprite's head (sprite uses setOrigin(0.5,1) — feet at py)
    32→  // Name label sits ~100px above feet; bubble goes above that
    33→  const cx = sprite.x;
    34→  const cy = sprite.y - 106 - bh - TRI_H; // top-left y of box
    35→
    36→  // ── Graphics (background + pointer) ──────────────────────────────────────
    37→  const gfx = scene.add.graphics().setDepth(20);
    38→
    39→  // White rounded rect
    40→  gfx.fillStyle(0xffffff, 0.92);
    41→  gfx.fillRoundedRect(cx - bw / 2, cy, bw, bh, BUBBLE_R);
    42→
    43→  // Subtle border
    44→  gfx.lineStyle(1, 0xcccccc, 0.8);
    45→  gfx.strokeRoundedRect(cx - bw / 2, cy, bw, BUBBLE_R * 2);
    46→  gfx.strokeRoundedRect(cx - bw / 2, cy, bw, bh, BUBBLE_R);
    47→
    48→  // Triangle pointer (pointing down to character)
    49→  gfx.fillStyle(0xffffff, 0.92);
    50→  gfx.fillTriangle(
    51→    cx - 6, cy + bh,
    52→    cx + 6, cy + bh,
    53→    cx,     cy + bh + TRI_H,
    54→  );
    55→
    56→  // Position text centred inside box
    57→  txt.setPosition(cx, cy + BUBBLE_PAD);
    58→
    59→  // ── Fade out & destroy ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    60→  scene.time.delayedCall(DISPLAY_MS, () => {
    61→    scene.tweens.add({
    62→      targets: [gfx, txt],
    63→      alpha: 0,
    64→      duration: FADE_MS,
    65→      onComplete: () => {
    66→        gfx.destroy();
    67→        txt.destroy();
    68→      },
    69→    });
    70→  });
    71→}
    72→

   239→
   240→  <script type="module">
   241→    import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './src/objects.js';
   242→    import { SimulationEngine } from './src/Engine.js';
   243→    import { Character } from './src/Character.js';
   244→    import { AIEngine } from './src/AIEngine.js';
   245→
   246→    // ── Walkable grid (mirrors scene.js) ──────────────────────────────────────
   247→
   248→    const GRID_COLS = 19;
   249→    const GRID_ROWS = 13;
   250→
   251→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   252→      const grid = [];
   253→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   254→        const r = [];
   255→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   256→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   257→        }
   258→        grid.push(r);
   259→      }
   260→      // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
   261→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   262→        const { tx, ty } = def.position;
   263→        if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
   264→          grid[ty][tx] = false;
   265→        }
   266→      }
   267→      return grid;
   268→    }
   269→
   270→    // ── Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) ─────────────────────────────
   271→
   272→    const CHARS_CONFIG = [
   273→      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,
   274→        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },
   275→      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,
   276→        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },
   277→      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 13, ty: 5,
   278→        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },
   279→    ];
   280→
   281→    // ── Engine setup ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   282→
   283→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   284→
   285→    const aiEngine = new AIEngine({
   286→      endpoint: '/api/llm',
   287→      model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   288→      decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   289→      onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
   290→        const targetName = decision.targetId
   291→          ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
   292→          : decision.targetTile
   293→            ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
   294→            : null;
   295→        pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
   296→      },
   297→    });
   298→
   299→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS, aiEngine });
   300→
   301→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   302→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   303→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   304→      }));
   305→    }
   306→
   307→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   308→
   309→    let paused = false;
   310→    let speed  = 1;
   311→    let lastTs = null;
   312→
   313→    // Event log (newest-first)
   314→    const log = [];
   315→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   316→    let logDirty = false;
   317→
   318→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   319→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   320→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   321→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   322→    }
   323→
   324→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   325→
   326→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   327→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   328→      paused = !paused;
   329→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   330→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   331→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   332→    });
   333→
   334→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   335→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   336→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   337→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   338→        btn.classList.add('active');
   339→      });
   340→    });
   341→
   342→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   343→      // Reset object states to defaults
   344→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   345→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   346→        if (!obj) continue;
   347→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   348→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   349→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   350→      }
   351→      // Reset sim clock
   352→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   353→      // Clear log
   354→      log.length = 0;
   355→      logDirty = true;
   356→      // Update badge classes immediately
   357→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   358→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   359→      }
   360→    });
   361→
   362→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   363→
   364→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   365→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   366→    ]);
   367→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   368→
   369→    function badgeClass(state) {
   370→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   371→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   372→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   373→      return 'other';
   374→    }
   375→
   376→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   377→
   378→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   379→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   380→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   381→      logDirty = true;
   382→    }
   383→
   384→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   385→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   386→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   387→      logDirty = true;
   388→    }
   389→
   390→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   391→
   392→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   393→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   394→      if (!obj) return;
   395→      const from = obj.state;
   396→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   397→      if (ev) {
   398→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   399→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   400→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   401→      }
   402→    };
   403→
   404→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   405→
   406→    function initObjectCards() {
   407→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   408→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   409→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   410→        card.className = 'object-card';
   411→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   412→        card.innerHTML = `
   413→          <div class="object-card-header">
   414→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   415→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   416→          </div>
   417→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   418→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   419→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   420→          </div>
   421→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   422→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   423→        `;
   424→        grid.appendChild(card);
   425→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   426→      }
   427→    }
   428→
   429→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   430→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   431→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   432→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   433→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   434→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   435→      if (!badge) return;
   436→
   437→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   438→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   439→
   440→      if (stateChanged) {
   441→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   442→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   443→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   444→
   445→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   446→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   447→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   448→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   449→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   450→        ).join('');
   451→      }
   452→
   453→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   454→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   455→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   456→      if (hasTimer) {
   457→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   458→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   459→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   460→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   461→        timerText.style.display = '';
   462→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   463→      } else {
   464→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   465→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   466→      }
   467→    }
   468→
   469→    function initCharacterCards() {
   470→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   471→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   472→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   473→        card.className = 'character-card';
   474→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   475→        grid.appendChild(card);
   476→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   477→      });
   478→    }
   479→
   480→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   481→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   482→      if (!card) return;
   483→
   484→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   485→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   486→        : char.targetObjectId
   487→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   488→          : '—';
   489→
   490→      // Hold countdown timer (shown while character is locked at an object)
   491→      let holdHtml = '';
   492→      if (char.action === 'interacting' && char.interactTimer > 0 && char.interactTimerMax > 0) {
   493→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - char.interactTimer / char.interactTimerMax) * 100));
   494→        holdHtml = `
   495→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   496→            <span>Hold</span>
   497→            <span class="char-value">${Math.ceil(char.interactTimer / 1000)}s</span>
   498→          </div>
   499→          <div class="stat-bar">
   500→            <div class="stat-fill hold-timer" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   501→          </div>
   502→        `;
   503→      }
   504→
   505→      // AI decision cooldown timer
   506→      let cooldownHtml = '';
   507→      if (aiEngine.enabled) {
   508→        const remaining  = Math.max(0, aiEngine._timers.get(char.name) ?? aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs);
   509→        const pct        = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - remaining / aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs) * 100));
   510→        const secRemaining = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000);
   511→        cooldownHtml = `
   512→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   513→            <span>AI next</span>
   514→            <span class="char-value">${secRemaining}s</span>
   515→          </div>
   516→          <div class="stat-bar">
   517→            <div class="stat-fill ai-cooldown" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   518→          </div>
   519→        `;
   520→      }
   521→
   522→      card.innerHTML = `
   523→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   524→        <div class="char-row">
   525→          <span>Action</span>
   526→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   527→        </div>
   528→        <div class="char-row">
   529→          <span>Position</span>
   530→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   531→        </div>
   532→        <div class="char-row">
   533→          <span>Facing</span>
   534→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   535→        </div>
   536→        <div class="char-row">
   537→          <span>Target</span>
   538→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   539→        </div>
   540→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   541→          <span>Mood</span>
   542→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   543→        </div>
   544→        <div class="stat-bar">
   545→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   546→        </div>
   547→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   548→          <span>Energy</span>
   549→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   550→        </div>
   551→        <div class="stat-bar">
   552→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   553→        </div>
   554→        ${holdHtml}
   555→        ${cooldownHtml}
   556→      `;
   557→    }
   558→
   559→    function renderEventLog() {
   560→      if (!logDirty) return;
   561→      logDirty = false;
   562→
   563→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   564→      if (log.length === 0) {
   565→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   566→        return;
   567→      }
   568→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => {
   569→        if (e.type === 'ai') {
   570→          const targetStr   = e.target   ? ` \u2192 ${e.target}` : '';
   571→          const dialogueStr = e.dialogue ? ` \u201c${e.dialogue}\u201d` : '';
   572→          return `
   573→            <div class="log-entry ai">
   574→              <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   575→              <span class="log-obj">${e.charLabel}</span>
   576→              <span class="log-transition">${e.action}${targetStr}${dialogueStr}</span>
   577→              <span class="log-tag ai">AI</span>
   578→            </div>
   579→          `;
   580→        }
   581→        return `
   582→          <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   583→            <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   584→            <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   585→            <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   586→            <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   587→          </div>
   588→        `;
   589→      }).join('');
   590→    }
   591→
   592→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   593→
   594→    function tick(ts) {
   595→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   596→
   597→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   598→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   599→
   600→        // Snapshot states before update
   601→        const snap = new Map();
   602→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   603→
   604→        // Advance simulation
   605→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   606→
   607→        // Detect auto-transitions
   608→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   609→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   610→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   611→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   612→          }
   613→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   614→        }
   615→
   616→        // Update character cards
   617→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   618→      }
   619→
   620→      lastTs = ts;
   621→
   622→      // Clock

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    67→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    68→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    69→      }
    70→
    71→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    72→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    73→        this._doWander(char);
    74→      }
    75→
    76→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    77→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    78→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    79→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    80→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    81→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    82→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    83→        }
    84→      }
    85→
    86→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    87→      char.update(deltaMs);
    88→    }
    89→  }
    90→
    91→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    92→
    93→  /**
    94→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    95→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    96→   */
    97→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    98→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    99→
   100→    if (event) {
   101→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   102→
   103→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   104→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   105→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   106→      if (obj && event.state) {
   107→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   108→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   109→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   110→        }
   111→      }
   112→
   113→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, holdMs);
   114→
   115→      if (event.speech) {
   116→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   117→      }
   118→
   119→      if (event.emoji) {
   120→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   121→      }
   122→    }
   123→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   124→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   125→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129→
   130→  _doWander(char) {
   131→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   132→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   133→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   134→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   135→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   136→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   137→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   138→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   139→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   140→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   141→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   142→            return;
   143→          }
   144→        }
   145→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   146→      }
   147→    }
   148→
   149→    // Random walkable tile
   150→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   151→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   152→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   153→      return;
   154→    }
   155→
   156→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   157→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   158→
   159→    let moved = false;
   160→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   161→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   162→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   163→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   164→      if (moved) break;
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    if (!moved) {
   168→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   169→    }
   170→  }
   171→
   172→  /**
   173→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   174→   */
   175→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   176→    const dirs = [
   177→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   178→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   179→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   180→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   181→    ];
   182→    for (const d of dirs) {
   183→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   184→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   185→      }
   186→    }
   187→    return null;
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   191→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   192→    const tiles = [];
   193→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   194→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   195→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   196→      }
   197→    }
   198→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   199→    return tiles;
   200→  }
   201→
   202→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   203→
   204→  getSimTimeString() {
   205→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   206→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   207→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   208→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   209→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   210→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   211→  }
   212→}

   184→        transitions: { use: { next: 'idle' } },
   185→      },
   186→    },
   187→  },
   188→  {
   189→    id: 'bonsai',
   190→    name: 'bonsai',
   191→    position: { tx: 11, ty: 8 },
   192→    interactMs: 5000,
   193→    state: 'idle',
   194→    states: {
   195→      idle: {
   196→        transitions: { use: { next: 'tending' } },
   197→      },
   198→      tending: {
   199→        speech: 'The bonsai looks healthy today.',
   200→        auto_next: { state: 'idle', after: 12 },
   201→      },
   202→    },
   203→  },
   204→];
   205→
   206→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   207→
   208→class ObjectInstance {
   209→  constructor(def) {
   210→    this.id        = def.id;
   211→    this.name      = def.name;
   212→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   213→    this.position  = def.position;
   214→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   215→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   216→    this.states    = def.states;
   217→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   218→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   219→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   220→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   221→  }
   222→
   223→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   224→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   225→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   226→  }
   227→
   228→  /**
   229→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   230→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   231→   */
   232→  interact(action = 'use') {
   233→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   234→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   235→    if (!tr) return null;
   236→
   237→    this.state = tr.next;
   238→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   239→
   240→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   241→    return {
   242→      objectId: this.id,
   243→      state:    this.state,
   244→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   245→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   246→    };
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /**
   250→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   251→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   252→   */
   253→  tick(deltaMs) {
   254→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   255→
   256→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   257→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   258→
   259→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   260→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   261→
   262→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   263→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   264→
   265→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   266→    return {
   267→      objectId: this.id,
   268→      state:    this.state,
   269→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   270→      auto:     true,
   271→    };
   272→  }
   273→}
   274→
   275→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   276→
   277→export class ObjectEngine {
   278→  constructor() {
   279→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  addObjects(defs) {
   283→    for (const def of defs) {
   284→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   285→    }
   286→  }
   287→
   288→  /**
   289→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   290→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   291→   */
   292→  tick(deltaMs) {
   293→    const events = [];
   294→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   295→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   296→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   297→    }
   298→    return events;
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  /**
   302→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   303→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   304→   */
   305→  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
   306→    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
   307→  }
   308→
   309→  getAll()   { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
   310→  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
   311→}

    50→    const r = [];
    51→    for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
    52→      r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
    53→    }
    54→    grid.push(r);
    55→  }
    56→  // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
    57→  for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
    58→    const { tx, ty } = def.position;
    59→    if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}
    65→

    68→export class CafeScene extends Phaser.Scene {
    69→  constructor() { super({ key: 'CafeScene' }); }

    73→  preload() {

    99→        frameRate: 6,
   100→        repeat: -1,
   101→      });
   102→
   103→      WALK_DIRS.forEach(({ key, start, end }) => {

   105→          key: `${name}_walk_${key}`,

   107→          frameRate: 8,
   108→          repeat: -1,
   109→        });
   110→      });
   111→    });
   112→

   118→      gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   119→      aiEngine: new AIEngine({
   120→        endpoint: '/api/llm',
   121→        model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   122→        decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,

   171→
   172→    // Show speech bubbles queued by the engine

   174→      if (char.pendingSpeech && char.sprite) {
   175→        showSpeech(this, char.sprite, char.pendingSpeech);
   176→        char.pendingSpeech = null;
   177→      }

   191→          y:       label.y - 40,
   192→          alpha:   0,
   193→          duration: 2000,
   194→          onComplete: () => label.destroy(),
   195→        });
   196→      }
   197→      this.engine.pendingEvents = [];

     1→/**
     2→ * /api/llm — Vercel serverless proxy for OpenRouter LLM calls.
     3→ * Keeps the API key server-side. The client sends the same Anthropic-style
     4→ * messages payload; we forward it to OpenRouter and relay the response.
     5→ */
     6→
     7→export default async function handler(req, res) {
     8→  // CORS headers for same-origin fetch from the static frontend
     9→  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
    10→  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');
    11→  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
    12→
    13→  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    14→    return res.status(200).end();
    15→  }
    16→
    17→  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    18→    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });
    19→  }
    20→
    21→  const apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
    22→  if (!apiKey) {
    23→    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'OPENROUTER_API_KEY not configured' });
    24→  }
    25→
    26→  try {
    27→    const { model, max_tokens, system, messages } = req.body;
    28→
    29→    // Use a cheap, fast model by default
    30→    const resolvedModel = model || 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku';
    31→
    32→    // OpenRouter uses OpenAI-compatible chat completions format
    33→    const openRouterMessages = [];
    34→    if (system) {
    35→      openRouterMessages.push({ role: 'system', content: system });
    36→    }
    37→    if (messages) {
    38→      openRouterMessages.push(...messages);
    39→    }
    40→
    41→    const response = await fetch('https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions', {
    42→      method: 'POST',
    43→      headers: {
    44→        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    45→        'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    46→        'HTTP-Referer': 'https://ai-aquarium-phaser.vercel.app',
    47→        'X-Title': 'AI Aquarium',
    48→      },

    50→        model: resolvedModel,
    51→        max_tokens: max_tokens || 256,
    52→        messages: openRouterMessages,
    53→      }),
    54→    });
    55→
    56→    if (!response.ok) {
    57→      const errorText = await response.text();
    58→      console.error(`OpenRouter error: ${response.status}`, errorText);
    59→      return res.status(response.status).json({ error: 'LLM request failed', detail: errorText });
    60→    }

Perfect! Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the codebase. Let me create a detailed report for you.

## Comprehensive Codebase Exploration Report

### Project Overview

This is an **AI Aquarium** - a cozy Japanese home simulation with LLM-driven character AI using Phaser 3. The architecture consists of:

1. **AIEngine.js** - LLM decision engine for character behavior
2. **Character.js** - Tile-based characters with A* pathfinding
3. **Engine.js** (SimulationEngine) - Core simulation loop
4. **objects.js** - Interactive object state machines
5. **speechBubble.js** - Speech bubble rendering
6. **scene.js** - Main Phaser scene
7. **debug.html** - Standalone debug dashboard
8. **api/llm.js** - Vercel serverless proxy

---

## 1. AIEngine.js (Complete Content)

**Path:** `/home/gem/project/src/AIEngine.js`

This is the core LLM-driven decision engine. Key features:

```javascript
/**
 * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
 *
 * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
 * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
 *
 * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
 *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
 *
 * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
 * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
 *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
 *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
 *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
 *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
 *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
 *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
 *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
 */
```

**Constructor config:**
- `endpoint` (string|null) - LLM API endpoint URL
- `apiKey` (string|null) - Bearer token
- `model` (string, default: 'claude-sonnet-4-6') - Model ID
- `decisionIntervalMs` (number, default: 30,000ms) - Decision polling interval
- `onDecision` (function|null) - Callback when decision is made

**Key Methods:**

- `update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState)` - Called each frame
  - Manages per-character cooldown timers
  - Won't make decisions while character is interacting
  - Requests decisions at the interval rate

- `_requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState)` - Async LLM call
  - Gathers nearby objects within 8-tile radius
  - Gathers nearby characters within 8-tile radius (excluding self)
  - Builds a system and user prompt
  - Sends to LLM endpoint with Anthropic-style JSON request
  - Handles both Anthropic and OpenAI response formats

- `_applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState)` - Executes action
  - **move**: calls `character.moveTo(tx, ty)`
  - **interact**: finds adjacent walkable tile, sets `targetObjectId` and `pendingAction`
  - **idle**: sets character's `wanderTimer` to one full decision interval
  - **talk**: moves character to adjacent tile of target character, sets `pendingSpeech` on target, pushes conversation event

**Talk Action Implementation (Lines 171-194):**
```javascript
case 'talk': {
  const target = characters.find(c => c.name === decision.targetCharacter);
  if (target) {
    // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
    const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
    if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
      // Character B responds when A arrives
      if (decision.targetDialogue) {
        target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
      }
      // Queue conversation event for the debug log
      if (simState?.pushEvent) {
        simState.pushEvent({
          type: 'conversation',
          speakerLabel: character.label,
          targetLabel: target.label,
          dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
          response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
        });
      }
    }
  }
  break;
}
```

## 2. Talk Action Implementation - Key Patterns

### In AIEngine.js (Lines 78-85): Nearby Characters Detection
```javascript
const nearbyCharacters = characters
  .filter(c => {
    if (c.name === character.name) return false;  // Exclude self
    const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;  // 8-tile radius
  })
  .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
```

This data is passed to the LLM in the user prompt so the AI knows who's nearby.

### In Character.js (Lines 137-142): Speech Management
```javascript
// Optional dialogue driven by AI
this.currentDialogue = null;
this.dialogueTimer   = 0;

// Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
// Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
// Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
this.pendingSpeech = null;
```

### In Character.js (Lines 248-252): Dialogue Timer Update
```javascript
// Tick dialogue
if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
  this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
  if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
}
```

### In speechBubble.js: Speech Bubble Rendering
```javascript
export function showSpeech(scene, sprite, text) {
  // Creates a white rounded-rect bubble with text
  // Positions above sprite's head
  // Automatically fades out after 2.5s over 600ms
}
```

### In scene.js (Lines 173-177): Bubble Display Loop
```javascript
// Show speech bubbles queued by the engine
for (const char of this.engine.characters) {
  if (char.pendingSpeech && char.sprite) {
    showSpeech(this, char.sprite, char.pendingSpeech);
    char.pendingSpeech = null;  // Clear after showing once
  }
}
```

## 3. Character and WorldState - Related Files

### Character.js - Key Fields for AI

**Position & Movement:**
- `tx, ty` - Tile coordinates
- `px, py` - Computed pixel positions
- `path` - Array of next tiles to walk through
- `moveProgress` - 0-1 interpolation between tiles
- `action` - 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'

**Interaction Targeting (for AIEngine):**
```javascript
// Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
this.targetObjectId = null;
this.pendingAction  = null;
```

**Personality Stats:**
```javascript
this.mood   = 100;   // 0–100, passed to LLM
this.energy = 100;   // 0–100, passed to LLM
```

**Perception Method:**
```javascript
getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
  return objects.filter(obj => {
    const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
    const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
    return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
  });
}
```

```javascript
this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();  // Manages all interactive objects

// Methods passed to AIEngine:
// - findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) - returns first walkable tile adjacent to position
// - pushEvent(ev) - queues event for scene (conversations logged here)
```

**Accessible via Engine:**
```javascript

simState.getSimTimeString()             // "8:30 AM" format
```

## 4. Debug Page Implementation

**Path:** `/home/gem/project/debug.html`

### Architecture:
- Standalone HTML/JavaScript dashboard (not Phaser-dependent)
- Uses same `SimulationEngine`, `AIEngine`, `Character`, `ObjectEngine` classes
- Real-time UI updates without Phaser rendering

### Key Features:

**Object Cards Grid:**
- Shows all 10 objects (stove, fridge, tea set, kotatsu, TV, bookshelf, desk, bed, easel, bonsai)
- Displays current state with color-coded badges (idle, active, done, other)
- Shows auto-transition timer bars
- Interactive buttons to manually trigger state transitions

**Character Cards Grid:**
- Shows position, facing direction, action state
- Displays mood and energy stats with progress bars
- Shows target object they're interacting with
- Shows AI decision cooldown timer

**Event Log:**
- Newest-first chronological log
- Object state transitions with trigger type (auto/manual)
- AI decision logging showing: character, action, target, dialogue
- Colored tags for log type (auto/use/ai)

### Debug API Hook (Line 289):
```javascript
onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
  const targetName = decision.targetId
    ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
    : decision.targetTile
      ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
      : null;
  pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
}
```

The debug page listens to `AIEngine.onDecision` callback to log AI decisions in real-time.

## 5. Key Architectural Patterns

### Separation of Concerns:

| Module | Responsibility |
|--------|-----------------|
| **AIEngine** | LLM polling, prompt building, decision parsing |
| **SimulationEngine** | Core loop, event queue, object/character ticking |
| **Character** | Movement (A* pathfinding), animation state, stats |
| **ObjectEngine** | State machine transitions, timers |
| **Scene** | Phaser rendering, sprite/text sync, event visualization |

### Data Flow for Talk Action:

1. **AIEngine._requestDecision()** - Collects nearby characters (8-tile radius)
2. **LLM prompt** includes nearby character list
3. **LLM response** includes `action: "talk"`, `targetCharacter`, `dialogue`, `targetDialogue`
4. **AIEngine._applyDecision()** - Finds target, moves current character adjacent to target, sets `target.pendingSpeech`
5. **Character.update()** - Ticks dialogue timer
6. **Scene.update()** - Renders `pendingSpeech` via `showSpeech()` when set
7. **speechBubble.js** - Creates white rounded bubble, auto-fades after 2.5s

### Nearby Character Lookup:

**In AIEngine (lines 78-85):**
```javascript

  })
  .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
```

This is passed to the LLM so it knows who to talk to.

## Summary

The codebase implements a sophisticated simulation where:
- **AIEngine** polls an LLM every 30 seconds per character
- Characters discover nearby objects/characters (8-tile radius) from their position
- The LLM responds with JSON actions: move, interact, idle, or **talk**
- For talk actions, the AI engine finds an adjacent tile to the target, moves the current character there, and queues speech for both characters
- Speech bubbles render via `showSpeech()` and auto-fade after 2.5 seconds
- A debug dashboard provides real-time visibility into all state machines, character positions, and AI decisions

Key Architectural Patterns\n\n### Separation of Concerns:\n\n| Module | Responsibility |\n|--------|-----------------|\n| **AIEngine** | LLM polling, prompt building, decision parsing |\n| **SimulationEngine** | Core loop, event queue, object/character ticking |\n| **Character** | Movement (A* pathfinding), animation state, stats |\n| **ObjectEngine** | State machine transitions, timers |\n| **Scene** | Phaser rendering, sprite/text sync, event visualization |\n\n### Data Flow for Talk Action:\n\n1. **AIEngine._requestDecision()** - Collects nearby characters (8-tile radius)\n2. **LLM prompt** includes nearby character list\n3. **LLM response** includes `action: \"talk\"`, `targetCharacter`, `dialogue`, `targetDialogue`\n4. **AIEngine._applyDecision()** - Finds target, moves current character adjacent to target, sets `target.pendingSpeech`\n5. **Character.update()** - Ticks dialogue timer\n6. **Scene.update()** - Renders `pendingSpeech` via `showSpeech()` when set\n7. **speechBubble.js** - Creates white rounded bubble, auto-fades after 2.5s\n\n### Nearby Character Lookup:\n\n**In AIEngine (lines 78-85):**\n```javascript\nconst nearbyCharacters = characters\n  .filter(c => {\n    if (c.name === character.name) return false;\n    const dx = c.tx - character.tx;\n    const dy = c.ty - character.ty;\n    return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;  // 8-tile radius\n  })\n  .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));\n```\n\nThis is passed to the LLM so it knows who to talk to.\n\n---\n\n## 6.      1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    54→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => ({ id: o.id, label: o.label, state: o.state }));
    77→
    78→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    79→        .filter(c => {
    80→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    81→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    82→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    83→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    84→        })
    85→        .map(c => ({ name: c.name, label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
    86→
    87→      const systemPrompt =
    88→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    89→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    90→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
    91→
    92→      const userPrompt =
    93→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
    94→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
    95→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
    96→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
    97→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
    98→        `Choose one action:
` +
    99→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   100→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   101→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   102→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_name", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   103→
   104→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   105→
   106→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   107→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   108→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   109→        model: this.model,
   110→        max_tokens: 256,
   111→        system: systemPrompt,
   112→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   113→      });
   114→
   115→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   116→
   117→      if (!res.ok) {
   118→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   119→        return;
   120→      }
   121→
   122→      const data = await res.json();
   123→
   124→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   125→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   126→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   127→              ?? null;
   128→
   129→      if (!text) {
   130→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   131→        return;
   132→      }
   133→
   134→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   135→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   136→    } catch (err) {
   137→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   138→    } finally {
   139→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   140→    }
   141→  }
   142→
   143→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   144→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   145→
   146→    switch (decision.action) {
   147→      case 'move':
   148→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   149→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   150→        }
   151→        break;
   152→
   153→      case 'interact': {
   154→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   155→        if (obj) {
   156→          // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   157→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   158→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   159→            character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   160→            character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        break;
   164→      }
   165→
   166→      case 'idle':
   167→        // Override wander timer — stay put for one full decision interval
   168→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   169→        break;
   170→
   171→      case 'talk': {
   172→        const target = characters.find(c => c.name === decision.targetCharacter);
   173→        if (target) {
   174→          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
   175→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   176→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   177→            // Character B responds when A arrives
   178→            if (decision.targetDialogue) {
   179→              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
   180→            }
   181→            // Queue conversation event for the debug log
   182→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   183→              simState.pushEvent({
   184→                type: 'conversation',
   185→                speakerLabel: character.label,
   186→                targetLabel: target.label,
   187→                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   188→                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
   189→              });
   190→            }
   191→          }
   192→        }
   193→        break;
   194→      }
   195→    }
   196→
   197→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   198→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   199→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    if (decision.description) {
   203→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   204→    }
   205→
   206→    if (this.onDecision) {
   207→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   208→    }
   209→  }
   210→}

   251→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   252→      const grid = [];
   253→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   254→        const r = [];
   255→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   256→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   257→        }
   258→        grid.push(r);
   259→      }

   261→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   262→        const { tx, ty } = def.position;
   263→        if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
   264→          grid[ty][tx] = false;
   265→        }
   266→      }
   267→      return grid;
   268→    }
