   283→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   284→
   285→    const aiEngine = new AIEngine({
   286→      endpoint: '/api/llm',
   287→      model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   288→      decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   289→      onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
   290→        const targetName = decision.targetId
   291→          ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
   292→          : decision.targetTile
   293→            ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
   294→            : null;
   295→        pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
   296→      },
   297→    });
   298→
   299→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS, aiEngine });
   300→
   301→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   302→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   303→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   304→      }));
   305→    }
   306→
   307→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   308→
   309→    let paused = false;
   310→    let speed  = 1;
   311→    let lastTs = null;
   312→
   313→    // Event log (newest-first)
   314→    const log = [];
   315→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   316→    let logDirty = false;
   317→
   318→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   319→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   320→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   321→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   322→    }
   323→
   324→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   325→
   326→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   327→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   328→      paused = !paused;
   329→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   330→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   331→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   332→    });
   333→
   334→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   335→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   336→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   337→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   338→        btn.classList.add('active');
   339→      });
   340→    });
   341→
   342→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   343→      // Reset object states to defaults
   344→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   345→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   346→        if (!obj) continue;
   347→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   348→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   349→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   350→      }
   351→      // Reset sim clock
   352→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   353→      // Clear log
   354→      log.length = 0;
   355→      logDirty = true;
   356→      // Update badge classes immediately
   357→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   358→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   359→      }
   360→    });
   361→
   362→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   363→
   364→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   365→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   366→    ]);
   367→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   368→
   369→    function badgeClass(state) {
   370→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   371→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   372→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   373→      return 'other';
   374→    }
   375→
   376→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   377→
   378→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   379→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   380→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   381→      logDirty = true;
   382→    }
   383→
   384→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   385→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   386→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   387→      logDirty = true;
   388→    }
   389→
   390→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   391→
   392→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   393→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   394→      if (!obj) return;
   395→      const from = obj.state;
   396→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   397→      if (ev) {
   398→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   399→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   400→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   401→      }
   402→    };
   403→
   404→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   405→
   406→    function initObjectCards() {
   407→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   408→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   409→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   410→        card.className = 'object-card';
   411→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   412→        card.innerHTML = `
   413→          <div class="object-card-header">
   414→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   415→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   416→          </div>
   417→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   418→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   419→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   420→          </div>
   421→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   422→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   423→        `;
   424→        grid.appendChild(card);
   425→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   426→      }
   427→    }
   428→
   429→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   430→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   431→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   432→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   433→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   434→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   435→      if (!badge) return;
   436→
   437→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   438→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   439→
   440→      if (stateChanged) {
   441→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   442→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   443→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   444→
   445→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   446→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   447→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   448→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   449→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   450→        ).join('');
   451→      }
   452→
   453→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   454→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   455→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   456→      if (hasTimer) {
   457→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   458→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   459→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   460→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   461→        timerText.style.display = '';
   462→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   463→      } else {
   464→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   465→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   466→      }
   467→    }
   468→
   469→    function initCharacterCards() {
   470→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   471→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   472→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   473→        card.className = 'character-card';
   474→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   475→        grid.appendChild(card);
   476→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   477→      });
   478→    }
   479→
   480→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   481→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   482→      if (!card) return;
   483→
   484→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   485→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   486→        : char.targetObjectId
   487→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   488→          : '—';
   489→
   490→      // Hold countdown timer (shown while character is locked at an object)
   491→      let holdHtml = '';
   492→      if (char.action === 'interacting' && char.interactTimer > 0 && char.interactTimerMax > 0) {
   493→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - char.interactTimer / char.interactTimerMax) * 100));
   494→        holdHtml = `
   495→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   496→            <span>Hold</span>
   497→            <span class="char-value">${Math.ceil(char.interactTimer / 1000)}s</span>
   498→          </div>
   499→          <div class="stat-bar">
   500→            <div class="stat-fill hold-timer" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   501→          </div>
   502→        `;
   503→      }
   504→
   505→      // AI decision cooldown timer
   506→      let cooldownHtml = '';
   507→      if (aiEngine.enabled) {
   508→        const remaining  = Math.max(0, aiEngine._timers.get(char.name) ?? aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs);
   509→        const pct        = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - remaining / aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs) * 100));
   510→        const secRemaining = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000);
   511→        cooldownHtml = `
   512→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   513→            <span>AI next</span>
   514→            <span class="char-value">${secRemaining}s</span>
   515→          </div>
   516→          <div class="stat-bar">
   517→            <div class="stat-fill ai-cooldown" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   518→          </div>
   519→        `;
   520→      }
   521→
   522→      card.innerHTML = `
   523→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   524→        <div class="char-row">
   525→          <span>Action</span>
   526→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   527→        </div>
   528→        <div class="char-row">
   529→          <span>Position</span>
   530→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   531→        </div>
   532→        <div class="char-row">
   533→          <span>Facing</span>
   534→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   535→        </div>
   536→        <div class="char-row">
   537→          <span>Target</span>
   538→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   539→        </div>
   540→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   541→          <span>Mood</span>
   542→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   543→        </div>
   544→        <div class="stat-bar">
   545→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   546→        </div>
   547→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   548→          <span>Energy</span>
   549→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   550→        </div>
   551→        <div class="stat-bar">
   552→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   553→        </div>
   554→        ${holdHtml}
   555→        ${cooldownHtml}
   556→      `;
   557→    }
   558→
   559→    function renderEventLog() {
   560→      if (!logDirty) return;
   561→      logDirty = false;
   562→
   563→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   564→      if (log.length === 0) {
   565→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   566→        return;
   567→      }
   568→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => {
   569→        if (e.type === 'ai') {
   570→          const targetStr   = e.target   ? ` \u2192 ${e.target}` : '';
   571→          const dialogueStr = e.dialogue ? ` \u201c${e.dialogue}\u201d` : '';
   572→          return `
   573→            <div class="log-entry ai">
   574→              <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   575→              <span class="log-obj">${e.charLabel}</span>
   576→              <span class="log-transition">${e.action}${targetStr}${dialogueStr}</span>
   577→              <span class="log-tag ai">AI</span>
   578→            </div>
   579→          `;
   580→        }
   581→        return `
   582→          <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   583→            <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   584→            <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   585→            <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   586→            <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   587→          </div>
   588→        `;
   589→      }).join('');
   590→    }
   591→
   592→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   593→
   594→    function tick(ts) {
   595→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   596→
   597→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   598→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   599→
   600→        // Snapshot states before update
   601→        const snap = new Map();
   602→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   603→
   604→        // Advance simulation
   605→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   606→
   607→        // Detect auto-transitions
   608→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   609→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   610→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   611→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   612→          }
   613→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   614→        }
   615→
   616→        // Update character cards
   617→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   618→      }
   619→
   620→      lastTs = ts;
   621→
   622→      // Clock
   623→      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();
   624→
   625→      // Event log (only when dirty)
   626→      renderEventLog();
   627→    }
   628→
   629→    // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   630→
   631→    initObjectCards();
   632→    initCharacterCards();
   633→    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   634→  </script>
   635→</body>
   636→</html>
   637→

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    67→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    68→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    69→      }
    70→
    71→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    72→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    73→        this._doWander(char);
    74→      }
    75→
    76→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    77→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    78→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    79→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    80→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    81→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    82→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    83→        }
    84→      }
    85→
    86→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    87→      char.update(deltaMs);
    88→    }
    89→  }
    90→
    91→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    92→
    93→  /**
    94→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
    95→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
    96→   */
    97→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
    98→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(char.targetObjectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
    99→
   100→    if (event) {
   101→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId);
   102→
   103→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   104→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   105→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   106→      if (obj && event.state) {
   107→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   108→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   109→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   110→        }
   111→      }
   112→
   113→      char.startInteraction(char.targetObjectId, holdMs);
   114→
   115→      if (event.speech) {
   116→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   117→      }
   118→
   119→      if (event.emoji) {
   120→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   121→      }
   122→    }
   123→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   124→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   125→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129→
   130→  _doWander(char) {
   131→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   132→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   133→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   134→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   135→        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile
   136→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   137→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   138→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   139→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   140→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   141→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   142→            return;
   143→          }
   144→        }
   145→        // All objects unreachable — fall through to random wander
   146→      }
   147→    }
   148→
   149→    // Random walkable tile
   150→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   151→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   152→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   153→      return;
   154→    }
   155→
   156→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   157→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   158→
   159→    let moved = false;
   160→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   161→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   162→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   163→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   164→      if (moved) break;
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    if (!moved) {
   168→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   169→    }
   170→  }
   171→
   172→  /**
   173→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   174→   */
   175→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   176→    const dirs = [
   177→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   178→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   179→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   180→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   181→    ];
   182→    for (const d of dirs) {
   183→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   184→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   185→      }
   186→    }
   187→    return null;
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   191→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   192→    const tiles = [];
   193→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   194→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   195→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   196→      }
   197→    }
   198→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   199→    return tiles;
   200→  }
   201→
   202→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   203→
   204→  getSimTimeString() {
   205→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   206→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   207→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   208→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   209→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   210→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   211→  }
   212→}

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n   129\u2192\n   130\u2192  _doWander(char) {\n   131\u2192    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely\n   132\u2192    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {\n   133\u2192      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();\n   134\u2192      if (objects.length > 0) {\n   135\u2192        // Shuffle and try each until one yields a reachable adjacent tile\n   136\u2192 139\u2192          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {\n   140\u2192            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;\n   141\u2192            char.pendingAction  = 'use';\n   142\u2192 160\u2192    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {\n   161\u2192      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];\n   162\u2192      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy)   180\u2192      { tx: tx + 1, ty },\n   181\u2192    ];\n   182\u2192    for (const d of dirs) {\n   183\u2192      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {\n ASSISTANTMESSAGE #49
Now I understand the situation better. Looking at the current code: 1. **AIEngine.js already has:** - Nearby characters detection (lines 78-85) - Talk action in the prompt (line 102) - `case 'talk'` in `_applyDecision()` (lines 171-194) 2. **However**, the debug page (`debug.html`) has an issue with the `onDecision` callback — when `action === 'talk'`, the `targetName` will resolve to `null` because: - It checks `decision.targetId` first (for interact) - Then `decision.targetTile` (for move) - But for talk, it would use `decision.targetCharacter`, which isn't being checked in the callback I need to look at how the `onDecision` callback in debug.html is handling the target name resolution, since it's missing the case for `targetCharacter`. Looking at the talk action in AIEngine.js, it's searching for the target character by name and then finding an adjacent walkable tile to approach them. But the debug callback doesn't account for this—it only checks `targetId` and `targetTile`, so when a talk action happens, `targetName` ends up null and the event log doesn't show what character was being talked to. I'm noticing an inconsistency in how dialogue gets displayed—the initiator's speech is set to `character.currentDialogue` while the target gets `pendingSpeech`, but `pendingSpeech` is what actually renders as a speech bubble in the scene. Let me trace through how these properties are used in the rendering logic to understand which one actually shows up in the game. Looking back at the issue description, the core problems are clear: the LLM prompt doesn't offer a talk action at all, there's no handler for it in `_applyDecision()`, and nearby characters aren't even included in the context the LLM sees when making decisions. But checking the current code, all three of these issues appear to already be resolved—nearby characters are being passed to the prompt, the talk option is listed as an available action, and there's a full handler for the talk case. The git history shows PR #5 added this functionality for FRG-206, so either this new issue FRG-219 was created after a partial fix, or there's still something broken that I need to dig into. Looking more closely at the talk implementation, I'm spotting a timing problem: the character moves to an adjacent tile first, but the code immediately sets the target's pending speech without waiting for the movement to complete. This could cause the dialogue to display before the character has actually arrived. Comparing this to the interact case, I see it handles this differently—it sets a `targetObjectId` and `pendingAction`, then lets the Engine's update loop detect arrival and trigger the action through `_handleObjectArrival`. But the talk case doesn't have an equivalent arrival handler, so the dialogue fires right away instead of waiting for the movement to finish. So the initiator's dialogue never shows as a speech bubble because it's being set to `currentDialogue` instead of `pendingSpeech`. I need to check how these two properties are handled in Character.js and scene.js to understand which one actually triggers the speech bubble display.

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}
   305→

    47→function buildWalkableGrid() {
    48→  const grid = [];
    49→  for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
    50→    const r = [];

    60→      grid[ty][tx] = false;
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→  return grid;
    64→}

The issue is that `pendingSpeech` displays immediately rather than waiting for the character to actually arrive at the adjacent tile, so the timing is off. Meanwhile, the initiator's own dialogue gets assigned to `character.currentDialogue` instead of `character.pendingSpeech`, which means it never triggers the speech bubble display at all since the scene only checks for `pendingSpeech`. ## Root Cause

1. The LLM prompt in `_requestDecision()` only offers 3 actions: move, interact, idle. No talk option.
2. `_applyDecision()` has no `case 'talk'` handler.
3. Nearby characters are not in the prompt context — only objects are listed.

## Fix Required

1. Add nearby characters to prompt context (name, position, current action).
2. Add talk action option to the prompt.
3. Add `case 'talk'` in `_applyDecision()`: move toward target character, set dialogue.
4. Talk should create a brief exchange — initiator says something via speech bubble.
